it&rsquo;s really a John Hancock</a></span><span>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span><a class="c2" href="#h.1eqde71a4idx">195</a></span></p><p class="c0 c16"><span class="c5"></span></p><p class="c0 c16"><span class="c5"></span></p><p class="c0 c16"><span class="c5"></span></p><p class="c0 c16"><span class="c5"></span></p><p class="c0 c16"><span class="c5"></span></p><p class="c0 c16"><span class="c5"></span></p><p class="c0 c16"><span class="c5"></span></p><p class="c0 c16"><span class="c5"></span></p><p class="c0 c16"><span class="c5"></span></p><p class="c0 c16"><span class="c5"></span></p><p class="c0 c16"><span class="c5"></span></p><p class="c0 c16"><span class="c5"></span></p><p class="c28"><span class="c139 c62 c85 c109">&#437;</span><span class="c85">ion</span></p><p class="c1"><span class="c5"></span></p><p class="c1"><span class="c5"></span></p><p class="c0 c16"><span class="c5"></span></p><p class="c1"><span class="c5"></span></p><p class="c28"><span class="c5">3/11/17</span></p><p class="c0 c16"><span class="c5"></span></p><h1 class="c38" id="h.hhwwzcg7j3wp"><span class="c53 c62 c61 c45 c104">We are in dire straights. &nbsp;</span></h1><p class="c0"><span class="c19">Over the course of the last four years I have watched civilization deteriorate to almost nothing before my very eyes. &nbsp;Not in the same way you have, not from things like censorship or Donald Trump; a much more nefarious force is at work here &hellip; it&rsquo;s closer to the things that you would describe as the Zombie Apocalypse and the Invasion of the Body Snatchers. &nbsp;Unfortunately for both me and for you, though, we are these zombies&hellip; our bodies being invaded by an unseen force throughout our entire lives and as that truth--one whose record pervades the hallowed verses of ancient scripture--finally comes to light with verifiable proof, this forces influence becomes ever so much more obvious. &nbsp;For years now, all around me, I&rsquo;ve seen and heard it speaking through the people around me; not just strangers, though there were tens of thousands of them involved, but also the people closest to me: my ex-wife my immediate family, even myself at times. &nbsp;</span></p><p class="c0 c16"><span class="c19"></span></p><p class="c0"><span class="c19">The proof, and the weapon delivered by God to hammer this invasion into submission is quite literally all around us--it&rsquo;s in every single word of every language, in every song and idiom about freedom ringing, and not only in the stories we watch on TV and in the movies and do not realize are the actualization of modern mythology, but also written into the actors names, proof that this story has been designed from before our births to save us from losing ourselves to &hellip; you&rsquo;ll never believe what it is we are fighting.</span></p><p class="c0 c16"><span class="c19"></span></p><p class="c0"><span>&ldquo;May you live in interesting times,&rdquo; one famous saying goes, and another to &ldquo;live long and prosper:&rdquo; that one combining with the Jewish priestly blessing in some kind of </span><span class="c27">awesome</span><span class="c19">&nbsp;linkage that might begin to open our eyes to the forces of causality and synchronicity at work as the worlds of scripture and &ldquo;the real&rdquo; That is why the Athenian lawmaker, Solon, decreed it a crime for any citizen to shrink from controversy.</span></p><p class="c0 c36 c16"><span class="c19"></span></p><p class="c0 c36"><span class="c19">That is why our press was protected by the First Amendment, the only business in America specifically protected by the Constitution, not primarily to amuse and to entertain, not to emphasis the trivial and the sentimental, not to simply give the public what it wants, but to inform, to arouse, to reflect, to state our dangers and our opportunities, to indicate our crisis and our choices, to lead, mold, educate and sometimes even anger public opinion.</span></p><p class="c0 c36 c16"><span class="c19"></span></p><p class="c0 c36"><span class="c19">This means greater coverage and analysis of international news, for it is no longer far away and foreign, but close at hand and local. It means greater attention to improve the understanding of the news as well as improve transmission. And it means finally that government at all levels must meet its obligation to provide you with the fullest possible information outside the narrowest limits of national security.</span></p><p class="c0 c36 c16"><span class="c19"></span></p><p class="c0 c36"><span class="c30">And so it is to the printing press, to the recorder of man&rsquo;s deeds, the keeper of his conscience, the courier of his news, that we look for strength and assistance. Confident that with your help, man will be what he was born to be, free and independent.</span><span class="c19">&nbsp;</span></p><p class="c0 c36 c16"><span class="c19"></span></p><p class="c0 c36"><span class="c19">John F. sure is the thing you want... before turning away at my attempt to classify myself as different from all those that came before me. &nbsp;You and I both know that we only have a story, a cartoon character if you will, to compare to--but even that story doesn&#39;t end with Jesus bringing freedom, Heaven, or Salvation... but rather his Kingdom Come before your eyes--the humble abode of </span><span class="c7 c15 c18">Lord Jesus</span><span class="c15 c18 c40">&nbsp;himself. &nbsp;I&#39;ve always taken offense to that word, and to be honest with you I&#39;ve shared numerous times all share a common attribute that I am quite certain is not only relevant but central to this day&#39;s message. &nbsp;Tying Caesar to the first Horsemen for instance are the famous words &quot;I came, I saw, I conquered&quot; and through that imagery and his riding into Rome to disband the senate and form an Empire we begin a pattern of the dissolution of representative governments in not only Rome but also France (and there, a tie in the name of the dictator to the Salt of the Earth... if you have a keen enough eye) and Germany where you see my initials in place of an element. &nbsp;So here I am telling you what I see as part of a hidden history of past now&#39;s, of a message about virtual reality and hidden technology being delivered to the world somehow ending up doing exactly the opposite of what it is that I intend to do. &nbsp;You see I am here to deliver to the world </span><span class="c23 c15 c18 c40">the right kind</span><span class="c6">&nbsp;of Iron Rod.</span></p><p class="c1"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c28"><span class="c6">I really don&#39;t like re-writing these explanatiions, it&#39;s very difficult to accurately record not only display: inline-block; margin: 0.00px 0.00px; border: 0.00px solid #000000; transform: rotate(0.00rad) translateZ(0px); -webkit-transform: rotate(0.00rad) translateZ(0px); width: 1.00px; height: 1.00px;"><img alt="" src="images/image16.gif" style="width: 1.00px; height: 1.00px; margin-left: 0.00px; margin-top: 0.00px; transform: rotate(0.00rad) translateZ(0px); -webkit-transform: rotate(0.00rad) translateZ(0px);" title="" /></span><span class="c47 c62 c59 c93 c45 c44">Today&#39;s date is 19 Kislev 5777, 12:04 AM, Mas or Mor?</span></h3><p class="c0 c16"><span class="c47 c34 c27 c18 c45 c44"></span></p><p class="c0"><span class="c34 c27 c18">It&#39;s hard to explain how these letter sequences stand out for me; it&#39;s probably some kind of subconscious filter--honestly, it&#39;s probably being handed to me telepathically each and every time. &nbsp;For instance; long ago I knew that I was the Fifth Adam, way before I had seen the confluence in modern art of Johnny 5 being alive, He-man linking to the fifth Hebrew letter, Voltron the same in Latin; and of course </span><span class="c3 c27"><a class="c2" href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=Uwzg7SYZKF0&amp;list=PLgYKDBgxsoMPrnVh3DiutJ2bZNwk6N_14">the Fifth Element</a></span><span class="c9">--this link between the numeric index of AD, Silicon, and Sinbad--I think it doesn&#39;t need to be expained more than that.</span></p><p class="c0 c16"><span class="c9"></span></p><p class="c0"><span class="c34 c27 c18">Standing out in bright song about &quot;</span><span class="c3 c27"><a class="c2" href="https://www.youtube.com/">wishing upon the same bright star</a></span><span class="c34 c27 c18">,&quot; (Somewhere Out There, Linda Rondstadt) is the link between the heart of the word Revelation and the name Fieval--who like the GAS hed of </span><span class="c3 c27"><a class="c2" href="https://www.youtube.com/">Live&#39;s narrative of my 2013 and 2014</a></span><span class="c34 c27 c18">&nbsp;was something of a tiny stoaway on a ship. &nbsp;That&#39;s the good old &quot;n,&quot; that I guess he owes &quot;civilization&quot; and &quot;revelation&quot; to--oh right, that&#39;s where we are right now. &nbsp;In my rules of macaroni-language, &quot;i&quot; is often expanded to &quot;is,&quot; you can see a good protoype for that in the laughter of </span><span class="c3 c27"><a class="c2" href="https://www.facebook.com/photo.php?fbid=10154283229013420&amp;set=a.10154283230918420&amp;type=3&amp;theater">Elisha and Elija</a></span><span class="c9">; so when I bring up Saint Nick, it&#39;s not that strange to see me echo &quot;n is CK.&quot; </span></p><p class="c0 c16"><span class="c9"></span></p><p class="c0"><span class="c34 c27 c18">Wishing upon that </span><span class="c3 c27"><a class="c2" href="http://www.metrolyrics.com/you-part-the-waters-lyrics-cake.html">lucky star</a></span><span class="c34 c27 c18">, like the little bay powered by the sun in his quest to turn Kentucky into something more like Kislev--maybe a mark for the actual time when we really do figure out that K comes right after J and there&#39;s more meaning behind that letter than simply it&#39;s link to Potassium, or a dual-minded &quot;</span><span class="c3 c27"><a class="c2" href="https://www.youtube.com/">person of time.</a></span><span class="c9">&quot; (Time Has Come, Europe) &nbsp;I have a special meaning for that letter that you might remember from MIB, it&#39;s a bright arrow pointing to &quot;El,&quot; who you might recall is the King of the Gods--and is focused in names like Israel and Larry Ellison. &nbsp;It&#39;s also prominent in the Hebrew name of Jesus Christ, El Elyon, which I read as &quot;the Y of now.&quot;</span></p><p class="c0 c16"><span class="c9"></span></p><p class="c0"><span class="c34 c27 c18">All of this stuff is probably not very meaningful to you--but to me it ties together not just hidden meaning tucked away in language, and a number of cartoons and stories that brighten the son&#39;s light.. it&#39;s also the reason I keep bringing up the connecting between King David (whose name I will remind you ties to </span><span class="c3 c27"><a class="c2" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Captain_EO&amp;sa=D&amp;ust=1513186496266000&amp;usg=AFQjCNFIsl_jpk3cOisg4e80_N0hosMWKQ">Captain EO</a></span><span class="c34 c27 c18">&nbsp;(which ties beautifully to the concept of &quot;dawn&quot; and the 40 days and years and miliseconds it takes now to see reference to time travel)... and </span><span class="c3 c27"><a class="c2" href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=NP3KxtDPWH0">DA VIDEO</a></span><span class="c9">&nbsp;that I am sure we will see, even if I have to make it here, myself) and David Letterman--whose name I see very clearly discussing the Jester of American PIe. &nbsp;</span></p><p class="c0 c16"><span class="c9"></span></p><p class="c0"><span class="c34 c27 c18">Leviticus, reverses that Fieval, the book is known at least tome... as &quot;</span><span class="c3 c27"><a class="c2" href="https://www.youtube.com/">the giving of the law</a></span><span class="c34 c27 c18">&quot; (Paradise City, Guns n&#39; Roses) it&#39;s the center of the Torah--and if you don&#39;t recall there&#39;s a Bible code pointing to that book from both ends of time... something like &quot;all languages point to Jerusalem. &nbsp;Generally when I see these &quot;letter names&quot; reversed, like the DA at the beginning of </span><span class="c3 c27"><a class="c2" href="http://matchbox20.bitbucket.io/sendgrid/happy4th.html&amp;sa=D&amp;ust=1513186496267000&amp;usg=AFQjCNG_xoUiKunhjC4GcEaObB1PMqroVw">DAVID</a></span><span class="c34 c27 c18">&nbsp;and the end of </span><span class="c3 c27"><a class="c2" href="https://matchbox20.bitbucket.io/archive.aweber.com/awlist4296878/MNcK4/h/Kurzweil_luminates_Zelda.htm">ZELDA</a></span><span class="c9">&nbsp;I read that as the person being... bent over backwards--maybe going out of their way, or simply being out of their element. &nbsp;Certainly, in a place where there&#39;s a &quot;giving of the law,&quot; I&#39;m both. &nbsp; And yet, here we are; seeing the &quot;rules of the game&quot; that I&#39;ve been given slowly trickling out towards ER--that one is &quot;everyone, really.&quot; &nbsp;RE, by the way, like in Creation and Revelation is short for &quot;reason,&quot; and any normal person can see the highlight of the word &quot;son&quot; in both those words. &nbsp;In really, and literally, that &quot;all&quot; ... the reason we are all saved by no other name--I think it has something to do with these guidelines. &nbsp;</span></p><p class="c0 c16"><span class="c9"></span></p><p class="c0"><span class="c34 c27 c18">Yoda, you seek </span><span class="c3 c27"><a class="c2" href="https://twitter.com/intent/follow?screen_name=yitsheyzeus">Yoda</a></span><span class="c34 c27 c18">. &nbsp;That&#39;s usually &#39;of&quot; but &quot;</span><span class="c3 c27"><a class="c2" href="https://twitter.com/intent/follow?screen_name=yitsheyzeus">hey</a></span><span class="c9">&quot; works.</span></p><p class="c0 c16"><span class="c9"></span></p><h1 class="c134 c60" id="h.iajc20xahwbg"><span class="c169 c62 c34 c27 c70 c45">Bible code</span></h1><p class="c60 c152"><span class="c47 c34 c21 c27 c18 c45">From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia</span></p><a id="t.6e818d2a134da10389c436056ff290c557217517" href="None"></a><a id="t.5" href="None"></a><table class="c90"><tbody><tr class="c26"><td class="c67" colspan="1" rowspan="1"><p class="c102"><span class="c113 c27 c18 c68">This is an </span><span class="c138 c33 c27 c18 c68"><a class="c2" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Page_history&amp;sa=D&amp;ust=1513186496270000&amp;usg=AFQjCNFkQ2Nz5g4xPDFiPAnBcRlzSXjeeQ">old revision</a></span><span class="c113 c27 c18 c68">&nbsp;of this page, as edited by </span><span class="c138 c33 c27 c18 c68"><a class="c2" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/User:Damonthesis&amp;sa=D&amp;ust=1513186496270000&amp;usg=AFQjCNGKZmcpigTzm3MUskmsIFr2s3z-PQ">Damonthesis</a></span><span class="c113 c27 c18 c68">&nbsp;(</span><span class="c138 c33 c27 c18 c68"><a class="c2" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/User_talk:Damonthesis&amp;sa=D&amp;ust=1513186496270000&amp;usg=AFQjCNFxP-NDkY3JMYgnLBWZOU39ALdWsw">talk</a></span><span class="c113 c27 c18 c68">&nbsp;| </span><span class="c138 c33 c27 c18 c68"><a class="c2" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Special:Contributions/Damonthesis&amp;sa=D&amp;ust=1513186496271000&amp;usg=AFQjCNGZQ72zYZTGkv6HHij6rAysn_QKFQ">contribs</a></span><span class="c113 c27 c18 c68">) at 05:06, 1 May 2013 (Malicious user). Previous revision</a></span><span class="c8">&nbsp;| </span><span class="c92 c33 c27 c18"><a class="c2" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bible_code&amp;sa=D&amp;ust=1513186496273000&amp;usg=AFQjCNEWMs69y4PtOU6xXlPit9Y40qKnoA">Latest revision</a></span><span class="c8">&nbsp;(</span><span class="c92 c33 c27 c18"><a class="c2" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title%3DBible_code%26diff%3Dcur%26oldid%3D552995533&amp;sa=D&amp;ust=1513186496274000&amp;usg=AFQjCNE3IfMxAPJ457NuOUCYw8eeiGg__A">diff</a></span><span class="c8">) | </span><span class="c92 c33 c27 c18"><a class="c2" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title%3DBible_code%26direction%3Dnext%26oldid%3D552995533&amp;sa=D&amp;ust=1513186496274000&amp;usg=AFQjCNGsbbk__PU3T_cvTA8Uaxou17eVrQ">Newer revision &rarr;</a></span><span class="c8">&nbsp;(</span><span class="c92 c33 c27 c18"><a class="c2" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title%3DBible_code%26diff%3Dnext%26oldid%3D552995533&amp;sa=D&amp;ust=1513186496275000&amp;usg=AFQjCNFSjPfp12A20_geSzp2SBoz6o99Dg">diff</a></span><span class="c8 c47 c45">)</span></p><p class="c159"><span class="c34 c27 c18 c87">The Bible code (</span><span class="c33 c27 c18 c76"><a class="c2" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hebrew_language&amp;sa=D&amp;ust=1513186496275000&amp;usg=AFQjCNHfbQkI2KkkjVZ4thfbV2fTtEHckw">Hebrew</a></span><span class="c34 c27 c18 c87">: &#1510;&#1508;&#1504;&#1497;&#1501; &#1489;&#1514;&#1504;&quot;&#1498;&lrm;&lrm;), also known as the Torah code, is a purported set of secret messages encoded within the Hebrew text of the </span><span class="c33 c27 c18 c76"><a class="c2" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Torah&amp;sa=D&amp;ust=1513186496276000&amp;usg=AFQjCNF-m6HyeRCSkIThaQx6URKAMXaztg">Torah</a></span><span class="c34 c27 c18 c87">. This hidden code has been described as a method by which specific letters from the text can be selected to reveal an otherwise obscured message. Though Bible codes have been postulated and studied for centuries, the subject has been popularized in modern times by Michael Drosnin&#39;s book </span><span class="c33 c27 c18 c87"><a class="c2" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Bible_Code_(book)&amp;sa=D&amp;ust=1513186496276000&amp;usg=AFQjCNGfgsUgHIAjfkB76txZGsRgMSGo-A">The Bible Code</a></span><span class="c34 c27 c18 c87">&nbsp;and the movie </span><span class="c33 c27 c18 c87"><a class="c2" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Omega_Code&amp;sa=D&amp;ust=1513186496276000&amp;usg=AFQjCNEIGSlD_JQHvJujHnkacC9O-xHabQ">The Omega Code</a></span><span class="c47 c34 c27 c18 c45 c87">.</span></p><p class="c60 c122"><span class="c34 c21 c27 c18">Many examples have been documented in the past. One cited example is that by taking every 49th letter of the </span><span class="c21 c33 c27 c18"><a class="c2" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Book_of_Genesis&amp;sa=D&amp;ust=1513186496277000&amp;usg=AFQjCNGrh1_OP19XMQ65hHfVn1VVcFNCeg">Book of Genesis</a></span><span class="c34 c21 c27 c18">&nbsp;starting with the first </span><span class="c21 c33 c27 c18"><a class="c2" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Taw&amp;sa=D&amp;ust=1513186496277000&amp;usg=AFQjCNHKbhv8mh7oO_1E98OfQ4y_lwlaZw">taw</a></span><span class="c34 c21 c27 c18">, the Hebrew word &quot;</span><span class="c21 c33 c27 c18"><a class="c2" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Torah&amp;sa=D&amp;ust=1513186496278000&amp;usg=AFQjCNF23UnhkT3kcaRyPBgYqmqfnG5E_g">torah</a></span><span class="c34 c21 c27 c18">&quot; is spelled out, the same happens in the </span><span class="c21 c33 c27 c18"><a class="c2" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Book_of_Exodus&amp;sa=D&amp;ust=1513186496278000&amp;usg=AFQjCNGX3wrmUOIiboFFXI5B5hhFJCgHug">Book of Exodus</a></span><span class="c34 c21 c27 c18">. The word &quot;</span><span class="c21 c33 c27 c18"><a class="c2" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Torah&amp;sa=D&amp;ust=1513186496278000&amp;usg=AFQjCNF23UnhkT3kcaRyPBgYqmqfnG5E_g">torah</a></span><span class="c34 c21 c27 c18">&quot; is spelled in reverse order, in the same manner, in the </span><span class="c21 c33 c27 c18"><a class="c2" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Book_of_Numbers&amp;sa=D&amp;ust=1513186496278000&amp;usg=AFQjCNGZLcAgiauS9o5S_-E1CiT1s4sqoA">Book of Numbers</a></span><span class="c34 c21 c27 c18">&nbsp;and the </span><span class="c21 c33 c27 c18"><a class="c2" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Book_of_Deuteronomy&amp;sa=D&amp;ust=1513186496279000&amp;usg=AFQjCNFK2OqvM6eoOnkmeiNLthUz2N9NUw">Book of Deuteronomy</a></span><span class="c34 c21 c27 c18">. The </span><span class="c21 c33 c27 c18"><a class="c2" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Book_of_Leviticus&amp;sa=D&amp;ust=1513186496279000&amp;usg=AFQjCNFFQj8YGtjsf6QEO7F79G7SRVlYBw">Book of Leviticus</a></span><span class="c34 c21 c27 c18">, contains the </span><span class="c21 c33 c27 c18"><a class="c2" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tetragramatton&amp;sa=D&amp;ust=1513186496279000&amp;usg=AFQjCNEXzlKXS7NeHEs9UIlsgARGnOWcNQ">Tetragramatton</a></span><span class="c34 c21 c27 c18">&nbsp;encoded using ELS with a skip of 7, with all four other books pointing towards it. The word Modern computers have been used to search for similar patterns and more complex variants, and published as a &quot;challenging puzzle&quot; in a peer-reviewed academic journal in 1994. Proponents hold that it is exceedingly unlikely such sequences could arise by chance, while skeptics and opponents hold that such sequences do often arise by chance, as demonstrated on other Hebrew and English texts.</span><span class="c33 c27 c61 c147 c18 c45 c44"><a class="c2" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title%3DBible_code%26oldid%3D552995533%23cite_note-1&amp;sa=D&amp;ust=1513186496280000&amp;usg=AFQjCNG30S03nj8E0VkuRStO6_LzFPYFnQ">[1]</a></span></p><p class="c0 c16"><span class="c33 c27 c61 c147 c18 c45 c44"><a class="c2" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title%3DBible_code%26oldid%3D552995533%23cite_note-1&amp;sa=D&amp;ust=1513186496280000&amp;usg=AFQjCNG30S03nj8E0VkuRStO6_LzFPYFnQ"></a></span></p><p class="c0"><span class="c34 c27 c18">Oh, right &quot;ER&quot; can also be &quot;and&quot; which honestly comes from a silly logical error, but you can see evidence that it&#39;s part of &quot;the Letterman&#39;s religion&quot; in Mr. Anderson, and </span><span class="c3 c27"><a class="c2" href="https://matchbox20.bitbucket.io/awlist4296878/Khraa/h/AM_ER_I_Come_Again_Mr_.htm">eternity</a></span><span class="c9">--and and and it&#39;s and. &nbsp;</span></p><p class="c0 c16"><span class="c9"></span></p><p class="c0"><span class="c9">I mean Y. &nbsp;You know: Latin, we live in a virtual world, rock n&#39;
